This is in contrast to some other\n        frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n        of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n        by dampening.                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n   305→            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt} 311→    \"\"\"\n   312→    + rf\"\"\"\n   313→    Args:\n   314→        {_params_doc}\n   315→        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3).           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n   456→                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   457→                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   458→                # has_complex = False\n        for p in group[\"params\"]:\n            if p.grad is not None:\n                has_complex |= torch.is_complex(p)\n                params_with_grad.append(p)\n           grads.append(p.grad)\n\n                state = self.state[p]\n                # Lazy state initialization\n                if len(state) == 0:\n                    if group[\"fused\"]:\n          (),\n                            dtype=_get_scalar_dtype(is_fused=group[\"fused\"]),\n                            device=p.device,\n                        )\n                        if r\"\"\"Implements Adam algorithm.\n\n    .. math::\n       \\begin{aligned}\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n                \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n                \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                                   \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(\n                device_params,\n                device_exp_avgs,\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt,\n                step_size,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            )\n\n\ndef _fused_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,  # Needed for consistency.\n    beta1: float,\n    beta2: float,\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,  # Needed for consistency.\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n) -> None:\n    if not params:\n        return\n    if differentiable:\n        raise RuntimeError(\"Adam with fused=True does not support differentiable=True\")\n\n    grad_scale_dict: DeviceDict = (\n        {grad_scale.device: grad_scale} if grad_scale is not None else {}\n    )\n    found_inf_dict: DeviceDict = (\n        {found_inf.device: found_inf} if found_inf is not None else {}\n    )\n\n    # We only shuffle around the lr when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    lr_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (\n        {lr.device: lr} if isinstance(lr, Tensor) and str(lr.device) != \"cpu\" else None\n    )\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n    for (device, _), (\n        (\n            device_params_,\n            device_grads_,\n            device_exp_avgs_,\n            device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n            device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n            device_state_steps_,\n        ),\n        _,\n    ) in grouped_tensors.items():\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n\n        device_grad_scale, device_found_inf = None, None\n        if grad_scale is not None:\n            device_grad_scale = grad_scale_dict.setdefault(\n                device, grad_scale.to(device, non_blocking=True)\n            )\n        if found_inf is not None:\n            device_found_inf = found_inf_dict.setdefault(\n                device, found_inf.to(device, non_blocking=True)\n            )\n        if lr_dict is not None and device not in lr_dict:\n            lr_dict[device] = lr.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n            lr = lr_dict[device]\n        torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n        func = torch._fused_adam_ if not decoupled_weight_decay else torch._fused_adamw_\n        func(\n            device_params,\n            device_grads,\n            device_exp_avgs,\n            device_exp_avg_sqs,\n            device_max_exp_avg_sqs,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            device_state_steps,\n            amsgrad=amsgrad,\n            lr=lr,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            beta1=beta1,\n            beta2=beta2,\n            weight_decay=weight_decay,\n            eps=eps,\n            maximize=maximize,\n            grad_scale=device_grad_scale,\n            found_inf=device_found_inf,\n        )\n        if device_found_inf is not None:\n            torch._foreach_sub_(\n                device_state_steps, [device_found_inf] * len(device_state_steps)\n            )\n\n\n@_disable_dynamo_if_unsupported(single_tensor_fn=_single_tensor_adam)\ndef adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    # One notable side effect\n   243→        of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n   244→        by dampening. group.setdefault(\"differentiable\", False)\n   122→            group.setdefault(\"decoupled_weight_decay\", False)\n   123→            fused = group.setdefault(\"fused\", None)\n   124→            for p in group[\"params\"]:\n   125→                p_state = self.state.get(p, [])\n   126→                if len(p_state) != 0 and not torch.is_tensor(p_state[\"step\"]):\n   127→                    step_val = float(p_state[\"step\"])\n   128→                    p_state[\"step\"] = (\n   129→                        torch.tensor(\n   130→                            step_val,\n   131→                            dtype=_get_scalar_dtype(is_fused=fused),\n   132→                            device=p.device,\n   133→                        )\n   134→                        if group[\"capturable\"] or group[\"fused\"]\n   135→                        else torch.tensor(step_val, dtype=_get_scalar_dtype())\n   136→                    )\n   137→\n   138→    def _init_group(\n   139→        self,\n   140→        group,\n   141→        params_with_grad,\n   142→        grads,\n   143→        exp_avgs,\n   144→        exp_avg_sqs,\n   145→        max_exp_avg_sqs,\n   146→        state_steps,\n   147→    ):\n   148→        has_complex = False\n   149→        for p in group[\"params\"]:\n   150→            if p.grad is not None:\n   151→                has_complex |= torch.is_complex(p)\n   152→                params_with_grad.append(p)\n   153→                if p.grad.is_sparse:\n   154→                    raise RuntimeError(\n   155→                        \"Adam does not support sparse gradients, please consider SparseAdam instead\"\n   156→                    )\n   157→                grads.append(p.grad)\n   158→\n   159→                state = self.state[p]\n   160→                # Lazy state initialization\n   161→                if len(state) == 0:\n   162→                    if group[\"fused\"]:\n   163→                        _device_dtype_check_for_fused(p)\n   164→                    # note(crcrpar): [special device hosting for step]\n   165→                    # Deliberately host `step` on CPU if both capturable and fused are off.\n   166→                    # This is because kernel launches are costly on CUDA and XLA.\n   167→                    state[\"step\"] = (\n   168→                        torch.zeros(\n   169→                            (),\n   170→                            dtype=_get_scalar_dtype(is_fused=group[\"fused\"]),\n   171→                            device=p.device,\n   172→                        )\n   173→                        if group[\"capturable\"] or group[\"fused\"]\n   174→                        else torch.tensor(0.0, dtype=_get_scalar_dtype())\n   175→                    )\n   176→                    # Exponential moving average of gradient values\n   177→                    state[\"exp_avg\"] = torch.zeros_like(\n   178→                        p, memory_format=torch.preserve_format\n   179→                    )\n   180→                    # Exponential moving average of squared gradient values\n   181→                    state[\"exp_avg_sq\"] = torch.zeros_like(\n   182→                        p, memory_format=torch.preserve_format\n   183→                    )\n   184→                    if group[\"amsgrad\"]:\n   185→                        # Maintains max of all exp. moving avg. of sq. grad. values\n   186→                        state[\"max_exp_avg_sq\"] = torch.zeros_like(\n   187→                            p, memory_format=torch.preserve_format\n   188→                        )\n   189→\n   190→                exp_avgs.append(state[\"exp_avg\"])\n   191→                exp_avg_sqs.append(state[\"exp_avg_sq\"])\n   192→\n   193→                if group[\"amsgrad\"]:\n   194→                    max_exp_avg_sqs.append(state[\"max_exp_avg_sq\"])\n   195→                if group[\"differentiable\"] and state[\"step\"].requires_grad:\n   196→                    raise RuntimeError(\n   197→                        \"`requires_grad` is not supported for `step` in differentiable mode\"\n   198→                    )\n   199→\n   200→                # Foreach without capturable does not support a tensor lr\n   201→                if (\n   202→                    group[\"foreach\"]\n   203→                    and torch.is_tensor(group[\"lr\"])\n   204→                    and not group[\"capturable\"]\n   205→                ):\n   206→                    raise RuntimeError(\n   207→                        \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n   208→                    )\n   209→\n   210→                state_steps.append(state[\"step\"])\n   211→        return has_complex\n   212→\n   213→    @_use_grad_for_differentiable\n   214→    def step(self, closure=None):\n   215→        \"\"\"Perform a single optimization step.\n   216→\n   217→        Args:\n   218→            closure (Callable, optional): A closure that reevaluates the model\n   219→                and returns the loss.\n   220→        \"\"\"\n   221→        self._cuda_graph_capture_health_check()\n   222→\n   223→        loss = None\n   224→        if closure is not None:\n   225→            with torch.enable_grad():\n   226→                loss = closure()\n   227→\n   228→        for group in self.param_groups:\n   229→            params_with_grad: list[Tensor] = []\n   230→            grads: list[Tensor] = []\n   231→            exp_avgs: list[Tensor] = []\n   232→            exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor] = []\n   233→            max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor] = []\n   234→            state_steps: list[Tensor] = []\n   235→            beta1, beta2 = group[\"betas\"]\n   236→\n   237→            has_complex = 243→                max_exp_avg_sqs,\n   244→                state_steps,\n   245→            )\n   246→\n   247→            adam(\n   248→                params_with_grad,\n   249→                grads,\n   250→                exp_avgs,\n   251→                exp_avg_sqs,\n   252→                max_exp_avg_sqs,\n   253→                state_steps,\n   254→                amsgrad=group[\"amsgrad\"],\n   255→                has_complex=has_complex,\n   256→                beta1=beta1,\n   257→                beta2=beta2,\n   258→                lr=group[\"lr\"],\n   259→                weight_decay=group[\"weight_decay\"],\n   260→                eps=group[\"eps\"],\n   261→                maximize=group[\"maximize\"],\n   262→                foreach=group[\"foreach\"],\n   263→                capturable=group[\"capturable\"],\n   264→                differentiable=group[\"differentiable\"],\n   265→                fused=group[\"fused\"],\n   266→                grad_scale=getattr(self, \"grad_scale\", None),\n   267→                found_inf=getattr(self, \"found_inf\", None),\n   268→                decoupled_weight_decay=group[\"decoupled_weight_decay\"],\n   269→            )\n   270→\n   271→        return loss\n   272→\n   273→\n   274→Adam.__doc__ = (\n   275→    r\"\"\"Implements Adam algorithm.\n   276→\n   277→    .. math::\n   278→       \\begin{aligned}\n   279→            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n   280→            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n   281→                \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n   282→            &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n   283→                \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n   284→            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n   285→                v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n   286→            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n   287→            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n   288→\n   289→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n   290→            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n   291→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n   292→            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n   293→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n   294→            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n   295→            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n   296→            &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n   297→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n   298→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n   299→            &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n   300→            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n   303→            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n   304→                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n   305→            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n   306→            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n   307→            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n   308→       \\end{aligned}\n   309→\n   310→    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n   311→    \"\"\"\n   312→    + rf\"\"\"\n   313→    Args:\n   314→        {_params_doc}\n   315→        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n   316→            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n   317→            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n   318→        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n   319→            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n   320→        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n   321→            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n   322→        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n   323→        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n   324→            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n   325→            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n   326→        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n   327→            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n   328→            (default: False)\n   329→        {_foreach_doc}\n   330→        {_maximize_doc}\n   331→        {_capturable_doc}\n   332→        {_differentiable_doc}\n   333→        {_fused_doc}\n   334→    .. 344→\n   345→def _single_tensor_adam(\n   346→    params: list[Tensor],\n   347→    grads: list[Tensor],\n   348→    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n   349→    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   350→    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   351→    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n   352→    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n   353→    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n   354→    *,\n   355→    amsgrad: bool,\n   356→    has_complex: bool,\n   357→    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n   358→    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n   359→    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n   360→    weight_decay: float,\n   361→    eps: float,\n   362→    maximize: bool,\n   363→    capturable: bool,\n   364→    differentiable: bool,\n   365→    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n   366→):\n   367→    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n   368→\n   369→    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n   370→        # this assert is due to JIT being dumb and not realizing that the ops below\n   371→        # have overloads to handle both float and Tensor lrs, so we just assert it's\n   372→        # a float since most people using JIT are using floats\n   373→        assert isinstance(lr, float)\n   374→        assert isinstance(beta1, float)\n   375→        assert isinstance(beta2, float)\n   376→    else:\n   377→        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n   378→        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n   379→\n   380→    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n   381→    # treating it as a scalar.\n   382→    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n   383→    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n   384→    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n   385→        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n   386→    else:\n   387→        beta1_dict = None\n   388→\n   389→    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n   390→        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n   391→        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n   392→        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n   393→        step_t = state_steps[i]\n   394→\n   395→        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n   396→        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n   397→            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n   398→            assert (\n   399→                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n   400→                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n   401→            ), (\n   402→                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n   403→            )\n   404→\n   405→        # update step\n   406→        step_t += 1\n   407→\n   408→        if weight_decay != 0:\n   409→            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n   410→                # Perform stepweight decay\n   411→                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n   412→            else:\n   413→                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   414→                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n   415→                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n   416→                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n   417→                    else:\n   418→                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n   419→                else:\n   420→                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n   421→\n   422→        if torch.is_complex(param):\n   423→            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n   424→            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n   425→            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n   426→            if amsgrad:\n   427→                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n   428→            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n   429→\n   430→        device = param.device\n   431→\n   432→        if beta1_dict is not None:\n   433→            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n   434→\n   435→            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n   436→            key = (device, dtype)\n   437→            if key not in beta1_dict:\n   438→                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n   439→                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n   440→                )\n   441→\n   442→            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n   443→        else:\n   444→            device_beta1 = beta1\n   445→\n   446→        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n   447→        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n   448→\n   449→        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   450→        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n   451→            if beta2.requires_grad:\n   452→                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n   453→                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n   454→                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   455→                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n   456→                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   457→                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   458→                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n   459→                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n   460→                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n   461→            else:\n   462→                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n   463→                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n   464→                )\n   465→        else:\n   466→            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   467→\n   468→        if capturable or differentiable:\n   469→            step = step_t\n   470→\n   471→            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   472→            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n   473→                if beta1.requires_grad:\n   474→                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n   475→                else:\n   476→                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n   477→            else:\n   478→                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n   479→\n   480→            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   481→            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n   482→                if beta2.requires_grad:\n   483→                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n   484→                else:\n   485→                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n   486→            else:\n   487→                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n   488→\n   489→            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n   490→            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n   491→\n   492→            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n   493→\n   494→            if amsgrad:\n   495→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   496→                if differentiable:\n   497→                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n   498→                else:\n   499→                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n   500→\n   501→                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n   502→\n   503→                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n   504→                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n   505→                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n   506→                denom = (\n   507→                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n   508→                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n   509→            else:\n   510→                denom = (\n   511→                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n   512→                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n   513→\n   514→            if differentiable:\n   515→                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n   516→            else:\n   517→                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n   518→        else:\n   519→            step = _get_value(step_t)\n   520→\n   521→            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n   522→            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n   523→\n   524→            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n   525→\n   526→            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n   527→\n   528→            if amsgrad:\n   529→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   530→                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n   531→\n   532→                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n   533→                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n   534→            else:\n   535→                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n   536→\n   537→            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   538→\n   539→        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n   540→        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n   541→            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n   542→\n   543→\n   544→def _multi_tensor_adam(\n   545→    params: list[Tensor],\n   546→    grads: list[Tensor],\n   547→    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n   548→    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   549→    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   550→    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n   551→    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n   552→    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n   553→    *,\n   554→    amsgrad: bool,\n   555→    has_complex: bool,\n   556→    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n   557→    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n   558→    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n   559→    weight_decay: float,\n   560→    eps: float,\n   561→    maximize: bool,\n   562→    capturable: bool,\n   563→    differentiable: bool,\n   564→    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n   565→):\n   566→    if len(params) == 0:\n   567→        return\n   568→\n   569→    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n   570→        if not capturable:\n   571→            raise RuntimeError(\n   572→                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n   573→            )\n   574→        if lr.numel() != 1:\n   575→            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n   576→\n   577→    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n   578→        if not capturable:\n   579→            raise ValueError(\n   580→                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n   581→            )\n   582→        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n   583→            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n   584→\n   585→    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n   586→        if not capturable:\n   587→            raise ValueError(\n   588→                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n   589→            )\n   590→        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n   591→            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n   592→\n   593→    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n   594→    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n   595→        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(\n   596→            supports_xla=False\n   597→        )\n   598→        assert all(\n   599→            p.device.type == step.device.type\n   600→            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n   601→            for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)\n   602→        ), (\n   603→            f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n   604→        )\n   605→\n   606→    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n   607→\n   608→    assert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n   609→\n   610→    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n   611→    # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n   612→\n   613→    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n   614→        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n   615→    )\n   616→\n   617→    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n   618→    # The Explore phase identified 10 common patterns that are repeated identically or near-identically across at least 5 optimizers.\n\nThese patterns include:\n- Empty list checks\n- Learning rate scalar conversion\n- Device/dtype grouping logic\n- Maximize flag handling with gradient negation\n- Weight decay application with memory reuse optimization\n- Step counter increments (with CPU efficiency optimization)\n- Complex number handling\n- Sparse gradient fallbacks\n- Capturable device validation\n\nBy extracting these patterns into a shared `torch/optim/_foreach.py` module, we can:\n- Reduce code duplication significantly\n- Improve maintainability (bug fixes apply to all optimizers)\n- Make patterns consistent across the optimizer suite\n- Enable easier addition of new optimizers\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Phase 1: Create `torch/optim/_foreach.py`\n\nCreate a new shared module with utility functions for common foreach operations:\n\n**Key utilities to extract:**\n\n1. **`_group_tensors_and_cast(grouped_tensors, tensor_count)`** - Helper to cast device-grouped tensors\n2. **`_apply_maximize_and_weight_decay(grads, params, maximize, weight_decay)`** - Apply both with memory reuse\n3. **`_increment_steps_efficient(state_steps, is_cpu_fallback_optimization)`** - Increment steps efficiently\n4. **`_ensure_capturable_devices(tensors, supported_devices)`** - Validate capturable device requirements\n5. **`_prepare_complex_tensors(params, grads, *state_lists)`** - Handle complex number conversion to real view\n\n**Module structure:**\n- Import necessary utilities from optimizer module\n- Define helper functions above\n- Document patterns and rationale\n- Add type hints for clarity\n\n### Phase 2: Refactor Optimizer Files\n\nRefactor 3+ optimizer files to use the shared module (SGD, Adam, Adagrad at minimum):\n\n**For each optimizer:**\n1. Add import: `from ._foreach import ...`\n2. Replace duplicated code in `_multi_tensor_*` functions with calls to shared utilities\n3. Preserve all external function signatures (public API compatibility)\n4. Update type: ignore comments as needed\n5. Ensure logic remains identical after refactoring\n\n**Priority order for refactoring:**\n1. **SGD** - Simplest _multi_tensor_sgd (applies most patterns: maximize, weight_decay, sparse check)\n2. **Adam** - Most complex; demonstrates all patterns\n3. **Adagrad** - Has sparse gradient fallback pattern to preserve\n\n### Phase 3: Maintain Backward Compatibility\n\n- All public function signatures remain unchanged\n- Internal _multi_tensor_* functions remain private (_prefix)\n- The step() method behavior is identical\n- Optimizer classes have same __init__ and public methods\n- State dict format unchanged\n\n### Phase 4: Implementation Details\n\n#### File: `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py`\n\nStructure:\n```python\n\"\"\"Shared foreach optimizer utilities for multi-tensor operations.\"\"\"\n\nfrom typing import cast, Optional, Callable, Union\nimport torch\nfrom torch import Tensor\n\n# Helper utilities for common patterns across optimizers\n\ndef _group_and_cast_tensors(...):\n    \"\"\"Safely cast grouped tensors to expected types.\"\"\"\n\ndef _apply_maximize_and_weight_decay(...):\n    \"\"\"Apply maximize negation and weight decay with memory reuse.\"\"\"\n\ndef _increment_steps_efficient(...):\n    \"\"\"Increment step counters with CPU optimization.\"\"\"\n\n# ... more utilities\n```\n\n#### Files to Modify:\n1. `/workspace/torch/optim/sgd.py` - _multi_tensor_sgd function (lines 378-471)\n2. `/workspace/torch/optim/adam.py` - _multi_tensor_adam function (lines 544-786)\n3. `/workspace/torch/optim/adagrad.py` - _multi_tensor_adagrad function (lines 388-495)\n\n#### Minimal Changes Approach:\n- Only extract patterns that appear in multiple optimizers\n- Don't over-engineer - use simple, direct helper functions\n- Keep functions focused on single responsibility\n- Preserve existing comments and logic flow\n\n### Phase 5: Testing Strategy\n\n1. **No new tests needed** - Existing test suite validates behavior\n2. **Verification approach:**\n   - Run existing optimizer tests to ensure functionality preserved\n   - Compare performance characteristics (foreach still works the same)\n   - Validate state dict loading/saving still works\n   - Spot-check one optimizer behavior before/after refactoring\n\n## Critical Files Identified\n\nFrom Explore phase analysis:\n- `/workspace/torch/optim/sgd.py` - _multi_tensor_sgd at lines 378-471\n- `/workspace/torch/optim/adam.py` - _multi_tensor_adam at lines 544-786\n- `/workspace/torch/optim/adagrad.py` - _multi_tensor_adagrad at lines 388-495\n- `/workspace/torch/optim/adadelta.py` - patterns present but lower priority\n- `/workspace/torch/optim/asgd.py` - patterns present but lower priority\n- `/workspace/torch/optim/optimizer.py` - Base class, contains _group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype\n\n## Existing Utilities to Reuse\n\nFrom `/workspace/torch/optim/optimizer.py`:\n- `Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype()` - Already does device/dtype grouping\n- `_to_scalar()` - Already converts learning rates to scalars\n- `_view_as_real()` - Already handles complex tensor conversion\n- `_get_capturable_supported_devices()` - Already exists, reuse in validation\n\nThese should NOT be re-implemented, only imported and composed.\n\n## Success Criteria\n\n1. ✓ `torch/optim/_foreach.py` exists with shared utilities\n2. ✓ SGD's _multi_tensor_sgd refactored to use shared module (reduces ~70 lines of duplicated logic)\n3. ✓ Adam's _multi_tensor_adam refactored to use shared module (reduces ~100 lines of duplicated logic)\n4. ✓ Adagrad's _multi_tensor_adagrad refactored to use shared module (reduces ~60 lines of duplicated logic)\n5. ✓ All existing tests pass\n6. ✓ Original optimizer APIs unchanged (step(), __init__(), state_dict())\n7. ✓ No performance regression\n\n## Alternative Approaches Considered (and rejected)\n\n1. **Single `_foreach_optimizer_step()` umbrella function** - Rejected because:\n   - Would require passing all optimizer hyperparameters as **kwargs\n   - Each optimizer has different state tensors (exp_avg_sq, momentum_buffer, etc.)\n   - Would obscure control flow and make debugging harder\n   - Better to extract specific reusable utilities\n\n2. **Create a ForeachOptimizer base class** - Rejected because:\n   - Current optimizers don't use inheritance for _multi_tensor_ functions\n   - Would require refactoring all optimizer class hierarchies\n   - Beyond scope of this refactoring\n   - Existing inheritance (SGD, Optimizer) shouldn't be disturbed\n\n3. **Gradual extraction of only top patterns** - Selected as the approach:\n   - Extract the 3-4 most commonly used patterns first\n   - Focus on high-impact, low-risk changes\n   - Can be extended in future PRs\n   - Maintains reviewer confidence with focused changes\n\n## Implementation Sequence\n\n1. Read and understand existing _multi_tensor_* implementations in detail\n2. Create `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` with carefully designed utilities\n3. Refactor SGD first (simplest case)\n4. Refactor Adam (most complex, validates approach works for complex optimizer)\n5. Refactor Adagrad (validates sparse gradient pattern extraction)\n6. Update imports in each file\n7. Run tests to validate all optimizers still work correctly\n8. Verify state dicts load correctly (backward compatibility)\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1565,"cache_read_input_tokens":50195,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1565},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"34faeb45-9508-40e5-ae8e-9b5b1f978c7d","uuid":"d75c8c56-e513-4da1-98d2-2139c9a24d39"}

The Explore phase identified 10 common patterns that are repeated identically or near-identically across at least 5 optimizers.\n\nThese patterns include:\n- Empty list checks\n- Learning rate scalar conversion\n- Device/dtype grouping logic\n- Maximize flag handling with gradient negation\n- Weight decay application with memory reuse optimization\n- Step counter increments (with CPU efficiency optimization)\n- Complex number handling\n- Sparse gradient fallbacks\n- Capturable device validation\n\nBy extracting these patterns into a shared `torch/optim/_foreach.py` module, we can:\n- Reduce code duplication significantly\n- Improve maintainability (bug fixes apply to all optimizers)\n- Make patterns consistent across the optimizer suite\n- Enable easier addition of new optimizers\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Phase 1: Create `torch/optim/_foreach.py`\n\nCreate a new shared module with utility functions for common foreach operations:\n\n**Key utilities to extract:**\n\n1. **`_group_tensors_and_cast(grouped_tensors, tensor_count)`** - Helper to cast device-grouped tensors\n2. **`_apply_maximize_and_weight_decay(grads, params, maximize, weight_decay)`** - Apply both with memory reuse\n3. **`_increment_steps_efficient(state_steps, is_cpu_fallback_optimization)`** - Increment steps efficiently\n4. **`_ensure_capturable_devices(tensors, supported_devices)`** - Validate capturable device requirements\n5. **`_prepare_complex_tensors(params, grads, *state_lists)`** - Handle complex number conversion to real view\n\n**Module structure:**\n- Import necessary utilities from optimizer module\n- Define helper functions above\n- Document patterns and rationale\n- Add type hints for clarity\n\n### Phase 2: Refactor Optimizer Files\n\nRefactor 3+ optimizer files to use the shared module (SGD, Adam, Adagrad at minimum):\n\n**For each optimizer:**\n1.
